      <div id="article-contents" class="article-grid-body"> 
       <p>This API is only available to authenticated members of the team's <a href="/en/rest/reference/orgs">organization</a>. OAuth access tokens require the <code>read:org</code> <a href="/en/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps">scope</a>. GitHub generates the team's <code>slug</code> from the team <code>name</code>.</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-teams" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-teams">List teams</a> </h3> 
         <p>Lists all teams in an organization that are visible to the authenticated user.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-teams--parameters"> <a href="#list-teams--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="list-teams--code-samples"> <a href="#list-teams--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/teams</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /orgs/{org}/teams'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">org</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'org'</span>
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 200 OK</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block">
          <pre><code class="hljs language-json">[
  {
    <span class="hljs-attr">"id"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"node_id"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"MDQ6VGVhbTE="</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"url"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.github.com/teams/1"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"html_url"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"https://github.com/orgs/github/teams/justice-league"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"name"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"Justice League"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"slug"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"justice-league"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"description"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"A great team."</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"privacy"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"closed"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"permission"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"admin"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"members_url"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.github.com/teams/1/members{/member}"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"repositories_url"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.github.com/teams/1/repos"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"parent"</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>
  }
]
</code></pre>
         </div> 
         <h4>Forbidden</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 403 Forbidden</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-a-team" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-a-team">Create a team</a> </h3> 
         <p>To create a team, the authenticated user must be a member or owner of <code>{org}</code>. By default, organization members can create teams. Organization owners can limit team creation to organization owners. For more information, see "<a href="https://help.github.com/en/articles/setting-team-creation-permissions-in-your-organization">Setting team creation permissions</a>."</p> 
         <p>When you create a new team, you automatically become a team maintainer without explicitly adding yourself to the optional array of <code>maintainers</code>. For more information, see "<a href="https://help.github.com/en/github/setting-up-and-managing-organizations-and-teams/about-teams">About teams</a>".</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /orgs/{org}/teams</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-a-team--parameters"> <a href="#create-a-team--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>name</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The name of the team.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>description</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The description of the team.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>maintainers</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>List GitHub IDs for organization members who will become team maintainers.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo_names</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The full name (e.g., "organization-name/repository-name") of repositories to add the team to.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>privacy</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The level of privacy this team should have. The options are:<br> <strong>For a non-nested team:</strong><br> * <code>secret</code> - only visible to organization owners and members of this team.<br> * <code>closed</code> - visible to all members of this organization.<br> Default: <code>secret</code><br> <strong>For a parent or child team:</strong><br> * <code>closed</code> - visible to all members of this organization.<br> Default for child team: <code>closed</code></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>permission</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Deprecated</strong>. The permission that new repositories will be added to the team with when none is specified. Can be one of:<br> * <code>pull</code> - team members can pull, but not push to or administer newly-added repositories.<br> * <code>push</code> - team members can pull and push, but not administer newly-added repositories.<br> * <code>admin</code> - team members can pull, push and administer newly-added repositories.</p> Default: <code>pull</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>parent_team_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The ID of a team to set as the parent team.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-a-team-by-name" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-a-team-by-name">Get a team by name</a> </h3> 
         <p>Gets a team using the team's <code>slug</code>. GitHub generates the <code>slug</code> from the team <code>name</code>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>GET /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-a-team-by-name--parameters"> <a href="#get-a-team-by-name--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="update-a-team" class="pt-3"> <a href="#update-a-team">Update a team</a> </h3> 
         <p>To edit a team, the authenticated user must either be an organization owner or a team maintainer.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>PATCH /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="update-a-team--parameters"> <a href="#update-a-team--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>name</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The name of the team.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>description</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The description of the team.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>privacy</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The level of privacy this team should have. Editing teams without specifying this parameter leaves <code>privacy</code> intact. When a team is nested, the <code>privacy</code> for parent teams cannot be <code>secret</code>. The options are:<br> <strong>For a non-nested team:</strong><br> * <code>secret</code> - only visible to organization owners and members of this team.<br> * <code>closed</code> - visible to all members of this organization.<br> <strong>For a parent or child team:</strong><br> * <code>closed</code> - visible to all members of this organization.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>permission</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Deprecated</strong>. The permission that new repositories will be added to the team with when none is specified. Can be one of:<br> * <code>pull</code> - team members can pull, but not push to or administer newly-added repositories.<br> * <code>push</code> - team members can pull and push, but not administer newly-added repositories.<br> * <code>admin</code> - team members can pull, push and administer newly-added repositories.</p> Default: <code>pull</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>parent_team_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer or nullable</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The ID of a team to set as the parent team.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="delete-a-team" class="pt-3"> <a href="#delete-a-team">Delete a team</a> </h3> 
         <p>To delete a team, the authenticated user must be an organization owner or team maintainer.</p> 
         <p>If you are an organization owner, deleting a parent team will delete all of its child teams as well.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>DELETE /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="delete-a-team--parameters"> <a href="#delete-a-team--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="delete-a-team--code-samples"> <a href="#delete-a-team--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X DELETE \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/teams/TEAM_SLUG</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'DELETE /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}'</span>, {

})

        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/projects</code></pre>

         <h3 id="check-team-permissions-for-a-project" class="pt-3"> <a href="#check-team-permissions-for-a-project">Check team permissions for a project</a> </h3> 
         <p>Checks whether a team has <code>read</code>, <code>write</code>, or <code>admin</code> permissions for an organization project. The response includes projects inherited from a parent team.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>GET /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/projects/{project_id}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/projects/{project_id}</code></pre>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="add-or-update-team-project-permissions" class="pt-3"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-project-permissions">Add or update team project permissions</a> </h3> 
         <p>Adds an organization project to a team. To add a project to a team or update the team's permission on a project, the authenticated user must have <code>admin</code> permissions for the project. The project and team must be part of the same organization.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>PUT /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/projects/{project_id}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/projects/{project_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="add-or-update-team-project-permissions--parameters"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-project-permissions--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> This API is under preview and subject to change. <a href="#add-or-update-team-project-permissions-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>project_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>permission</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The permission to grant to the team for this project. Can be one of:<br> * <code>read</code> - team members can read, but not write to or administer this project.<br> * <code>write</code> - team members can read and write, but not administer this project.<br> * <code>admin</code> - team members can read, write and administer this project.<br> Default: the team's <code>permission</code> attribute will be used to determine what permission to grant the team on this project. Note that, if you choose not to pass any parameters, you'll need to set <code>Content-Length</code> to zero when calling out to this endpoint. For more information, see "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#http-verbs">HTTP verbs</a>."</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \

         <h4 id="add-or-update-team-project-permissions-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>The Projects API is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the API may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-10-27-changes-to-projects-api">blog post</a> for full details. To access the API during the preview period, you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.inertia-preview+json</code></pre> ?? This header is <strong>required</strong>. 
         </div> 
        </div>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="remove-a-project-from-a-team" class="pt-3"> <a href="#remove-a-project-from-a-team">Remove a project from a team</a> </h3> 
         <p>Removes an organization project from a team. An organization owner or a team maintainer can remove any project from the team. To remove a project from a team as an organization member, the authenticated user must have <code>read</code> access to both the team and project, or <code>admin</code> access to the team or project. This endpoint removes the project from the team, but does not delete the project.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>DELETE /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/projects/{project_id}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/projects/{project_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="remove-a-project-from-a-team--parameters"> <a href="#remove-a-project-from-a-team--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead>

            <th>In</th>

           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr>

            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td>

           </tr>

         <h3 id="list-team-repositories" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-team-repositories">List team repositories</a> </h3> 
         <p>Lists a team's repositories visible to the authenticated user.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>GET /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/repos</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/repos</code></pre> 
        <div>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="check-team-permissions-for-a-repository" class="pt-3"> <a href="#check-team-permissions-for-a-repository">Check team permissions for a repository</a> </h3> 
         <p>Checks whether a team has <code>admin</code>, <code>push</code>, <code>maintain</code>, <code>triage</code>, or <code>pull</code> permission for a repository. Repositories inherited through a parent team will also be checked.</p> 
         <p>You can also get information about the specified repository, including what permissions the team grants on it, by passing the following custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types/">media type</a> via the <code>application/vnd.github.v3.repository+json</code> accept header.</p> 
         <p>If a team doesn't have permission for the repository, you will receive a <code>404 Not Found</code> response status.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>GET /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/repos/{owner}/{repo}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/repos/{owner}/{repo}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="check-team-permissions-for-a-repository--parameters"> <a href="#check-team-permissions-for-a-repository--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="check-team-permissions-for-a-repository--code-samples"> <a href="#check-team-permissions-for-a-repository--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/teams/TEAM_SLUG/repos/octocat/hello-world</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/repos/{owner}/{repo}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">org</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'org'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">team_slug</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'team_slug'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <h4>Response if team has permission for the repository. This is the response when the repository media type hasn't been provded in the Accept header.</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 204 No Content</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Not Found if team does not have permission for the repository</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 404 Not Found</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="add-or-update-team-repository-permissions" class="pt-3"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-repository-permissions">Add or update team repository permissions</a> </h3> 
         <p>To add a repository to a team or update the team's permission on a repository, the authenticated user must have admin access to the repository, and must be able to see the team. The repository must be owned by the organization, or a direct fork of a repository owned by the organization. You will get a <code>422 Unprocessable Entity</code> status if you attempt to add a repository to a team that is not owned by the organization. Note that, if you choose not to pass any parameters, you'll need to set <code>Content-Length</code> to zero when calling out to this endpoint. For more information, see "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#http-verbs">HTTP verbs</a>."</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>PUT /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/repos/{owner}/{repo}</code>.</p> 
         <p>For more information about the permission levels, see "<a href="https://help.github.com/en/github/setting-up-and-managing-organizations-and-teams/repository-permission-levels-for-an-organization#permission-levels-for-repositories-owned-by-an-organization">Repository permission levels for an organization</a>".</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/repos/{owner}/{repo}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="add-or-update-team-repository-permissions--parameters"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-repository-permissions--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>permission</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The permission to grant the team on this repository. Can be one of:<br> * <code>pull</code> - team members can pull, but not push to or administer this repository.<br> * <code>push</code> - team members can pull and push, but not administer this repository.<br> * <code>admin</code> - team members can pull, push and administer this repository.<br> * <code>maintain</code> - team members can manage the repository without access to sensitive or destructive actions. Recommended for project managers. Only applies to repositories owned by organizations.<br> * <code>triage</code> - team members can proactively manage issues and pull requests without write access. Recommended for contributors who triage a repository. Only applies to repositories owned by organizations. </p> <p>If no permission is specified, the team's <code>permission</code> attribute will be used to determine what permission to grant the team on this repository.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="add-or-update-team-repository-permissions--code-samples"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-repository-permissions--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X PUT \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/teams/TEAM_SLUG/repos/octocat/hello-world \
  -d '{"permission":"permission"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'PUT /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/repos/{owner}/{repo}'</span>, {

        <div> 
         <h3 id="remove-a-repository-from-a-team" class="pt-3"> <a href="#remove-a-repository-from-a-team">Remove a repository from a team</a> </h3> 
         <p>If the authenticated user is an organization owner or a team maintainer, they can remove any repositories from the team. To remove a repository from a team as an organization member, the authenticated user must have admin access to the repository and must be able to see the team. This does not delete the repository, it just removes it from the team.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>DELETE /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/repos/{owner}/{repo}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/repos/{owner}/{repo}</code></pre> 
        <div>

         <h3 id="list-child-teams" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-child-teams">List child teams</a> </h3>

         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>GET /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/teams</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/teams</code></pre>

         <h3 id="update-a-team-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#update-a-team-legacy">Update a team (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#update-a-team">Update a team</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>To edit a team, the authenticated user must either be an organization owner or a team maintainer.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> With nested teams, the <code>privacy</code> for parent teams cannot be <code>secret</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /teams/{team_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="update-a-team-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#update-a-team-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td>

            <td><code>name</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td>

           </tr>

            <td><code>description</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The description of the team.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>privacy</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The level of privacy this team should have. Editing teams without specifying this parameter leaves <code>privacy</code> intact. The options are:<br> <strong>For a non-nested team:</strong><br> * <code>secret</code> - only visible to organization owners and members of this team.<br> * <code>closed</code> - visible to all members of this organization.<br> <strong>For a parent or child team:</strong><br> * <code>closed</code> - visible to all members of this organization.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>permission</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Deprecated</strong>. The permission that new repositories will be added to the team with when none is specified. Can be one of:<br> * <code>pull</code> - team members can pull, but not push to or administer newly-added repositories.<br> * <code>push</code> - team members can pull and push, but not administer newly-added repositories.<br> * <code>admin</code> - team members can pull, push and administer newly-added repositories.</p> Default: <code>pull</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>parent_team_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer or nullable</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The ID of a team to set as the parent team.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

         <h3 id="delete-a-team-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#delete-a-team-legacy">Delete a team (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#delete-a-team">Delete a team</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>To delete a team, the authenticated user must be an organization owner or team maintainer.</p> 
         <p>If you are an organization owner, deleting a parent team will delete all of its child teams as well.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /teams/{team_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="delete-a-team-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#delete-a-team-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead>

            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_id</code></td>

         <h3 id="list-team-projects-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-team-projects-legacy">List team projects (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#list-team-projects"><code>List team projects</code></a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Lists the organization projects for a team.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /teams/{team_id}/projects</code></pre>

         <h4 id="list-team-projects-legacy-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>The Projects API is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the API may change without advance notice. To access the API during the preview period, you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.inertia-preview+json</code></pre> ?? This header is <strong>required</strong>.

         <h3 id="check-team-permissions-for-a-project-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#check-team-permissions-for-a-project-legacy">Check team permissions for a project (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#check-team-permissions-for-a-project">Check team permissions for a project</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Checks whether a team has <code>read</code>, <code>write</code>, or <code>admin</code> permissions for an organization project. The response includes projects inherited from a parent team.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /teams/{team_id}/projects/{project_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="check-team-permissions-for-a-project-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#check-team-permissions-for-a-project-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="add-or-update-team-project-permissions-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-project-permissions-legacy">Add or update team project permissions (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#add-or-update-team-project-permissions">Add or update team project permissions</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Adds an organization project to a team. To add a project to a team or update the team's permission on a project, the authenticated user must have <code>admin</code> permissions for the project. The project and team must be part of the same organization.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /teams/{team_id}/projects/{project_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="add-or-update-team-project-permissions-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-project-permissions-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> This API is under preview and subject to change. <a href="#add-or-update-team-project-permissions-legacy-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>project_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>permission</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The permission to grant to the team for this project. Can be one of:<br> * <code>read</code> - team members can read, but not write to or administer this project.<br> * <code>write</code> - team members can read and write, but not administer this project.<br> * <code>admin</code> - team members can read, write and administer this project.<br> Default: the team's <code>permission</code> attribute will be used to determine what permission to grant the team on this project. Note that, if you choose not to pass any parameters, you'll need to set <code>Content-Length</code> to zero when calling out to this endpoint. For more information, see "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#http-verbs">HTTP verbs</a>."</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="add-or-update-team-project-permissions-legacy--code-samples"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-project-permissions-legacy--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X PUT \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.inertia-preview+json" \
  https://api.github.com/teams/42/projects/42 \
  -d '{"permission":"permission"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'PUT /teams/{team_id}/projects/{project_id}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">team_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">project_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">permission</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'permission'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">mediaType</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">previews</span>: [
      <span class="hljs-string">'inertia'</span>
    ]
  }
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 204 No Content</code></pre>

         <h3 id="remove-a-project-from-a-team-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#remove-a-project-from-a-team-legacy">Remove a project from a team (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#remove-a-project-from-a-team">Remove a project from a team</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Removes an organization project from a team. An organization owner or a team maintainer can remove any project from the team. To remove a project from a team as an organization member, the authenticated user must have <code>read</code> access to both the team and project, or <code>admin</code> access to the team or project. <strong>Note:</strong> This endpoint removes the project from the team, but does not delete it.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /teams/{team_id}/projects/{project_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="remove-a-project-from-a-team-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#remove-a-project-from-a-team-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

  }
]
</code></pre>
         </div> 
         <h4>Resource not found</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 404 Not Found</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="check-team-permissions-for-a-repository-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#check-team-permissions-for-a-repository-legacy">Check team permissions for a repository (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Note</strong>: Repositories inherited through a parent team will also be checked.</p> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#check-team-permissions-for-a-repository">Check team permissions for a repository</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>You can also get information about the specified repository, including what permissions the team grants on it, by passing the following custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types/">media type</a> via the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /teams/{team_id}/repos/{owner}/{repo}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="check-team-permissions-for-a-repository-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#check-team-permissions-for-a-repository-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="check-team-permissions-for-a-repository-legacy--code-samples"> <a href="#check-team-permissions-for-a-repository-legacy--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/teams/42/repos/octocat/hello-world</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /teams/{team_id}/repos/{owner}/{repo}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">team_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,

  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>
})
</code></pre>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="add-or-update-team-repository-permissions-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-repository-permissions-legacy">Add or update team repository permissions (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#add-or-update-team-repository-permissions">Add or update team repository permissions</a>" endpoint.</p> 
         <p>To add a repository to a team or update the team's permission on a repository, the authenticated user must have admin access to the repository, and must be able to see the team. The repository must be owned by the organization, or a direct fork of a repository owned by the organization. You will get a <code>422 Unprocessable Entity</code> status if you attempt to add a repository to a team that is not owned by the organization.</p> 
         <p>Note that, if you choose not to pass any parameters, you'll need to set <code>Content-Length</code> to zero when calling out to this endpoint. For more information, see "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#http-verbs">HTTP verbs</a>."</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /teams/{team_id}/repos/{owner}/{repo}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="add-or-update-team-repository-permissions-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-repository-permissions-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>permission</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The permission to grant the team on this repository. Can be one of:<br> * <code>pull</code> - team members can pull, but not push to or administer this repository.<br> * <code>push</code> - team members can pull and push, but not administer this repository.<br> * <code>admin</code> - team members can pull, push and administer this repository. </p> <p>If no permission is specified, the team's <code>permission</code> attribute will be used to determine what permission to grant the team on this repository.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="add-or-update-team-repository-permissions-legacy--code-samples"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-repository-permissions-legacy--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X PUT \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/teams/42/repos/octocat/hello-world \
  -d '{"permission":"permission"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'PUT /teams/{team_id}/repos/{owner}/{repo}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">team_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">permission</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'permission'</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <h3 id="remove-a-repository-from-a-team-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#remove-a-repository-from-a-team-legacy">Remove a repository from a team (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#remove-a-repository-from-a-team">Remove a repository from a team</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>If the authenticated user is an organization owner or a team maintainer, they can remove any repositories from the team. To remove a repository from a team as an organization member, the authenticated user must have admin access to the repository and must be able to see the team. NOTE: This does not delete the repository, it just removes it from the team.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /teams/{team_id}/repos/{owner}/{repo}</code></pre> 
        <div>

         <h3 id="list-teams-for-the-authenticated-user" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-teams-for-the-authenticated-user">List teams for the authenticated user</a> </h3> 
         <p>List all of the teams across all of the organizations to which the authenticated user belongs. This method requires <code>user</code>, <code>repo</code>, or <code>read:org</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a> when authenticating via <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/">OAuth</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /user/teams</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-teams-for-the-authenticated-user--parameters"> <a href="#list-teams-for-the-authenticated-user--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--

       <h2 id="discussions"><a href="#discussions">Discussions</a></h2> 
       <p>The team discussions API allows you to get, create, edit, and delete discussion posts on a team's page. You can use team discussions to have conversations that are not specific to a repository or project. Any member of the team's <a href="/en/rest/reference/orgs">organization</a> can create and read public discussion posts. For more details, see "<a href="/en/organizations/collaborating-with-your-team/about-team-discussions">About team discussions</a>." To learn more about commenting on a discussion post, see the <a href="/en/rest/reference/teams#discussion-comments">team discussion comments API</a>. This API is only available to authenticated members of the team's organization.</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-discussions" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-discussions">List discussions</a> </h3> 
         <p>List all discussions on a team's page. OAuth access tokens require the <code>read:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>GET /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/discussions</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-discussions--parameters"> <a href="#list-discussions--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

          <thead> 
           <tr>

            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead>

            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          -->

            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td>

           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr>

            <td class="opacity-70">string</td>

           </tr>

         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <h4 id="list-discussions-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-a-discussion" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-a-discussion">Create a discussion</a> </h3> 
         <p>Creates a new discussion post on a team's page. OAuth access tokens require the <code>write:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p>This endpoint triggers <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/managing-subscriptions-and-notifications-on-github/about-notifications">notifications</a>. Creating content too quickly using this endpoint may result in abuse rate limiting. See "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#abuse-rate-limits">Abuse rate limits</a>" and "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/guides/best-practices-for-integrators#dealing-with-rate-limits">Dealing with abuse rate limits</a>" for details.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>POST /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/discussions</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-a-discussion--parameters"> <a href="#create-a-discussion--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#create-a-discussion-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>title</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The discussion post's title.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>body</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The discussion post's body text.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>private</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">boolean</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Private posts are only visible to team members, organization owners, and team maintainers. Public posts are visible to all members of the organization. Set to <code>true</code> to create a private post.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="create-a-discussion--code-samples"> <a href="#create-a-discussion--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/teams/TEAM_SLUG/discussions \
  -d '{"title":"title","body":"body"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'POST /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">org</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'org'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">team_slug</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'team_slug'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'title'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">body</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'body'</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <h4 id="create-a-discussion-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-a-discussion" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-a-discussion">Get a discussion</a> </h3> 
         <p>Get a specific discussion on a team's page. OAuth access tokens require the <code>read:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>GET /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-a-discussion--parameters"> <a href="#get-a-discussion--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#get-a-discussion-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>discussion_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="get-a-discussion--code-samples"> <a href="#get-a-discussion--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/teams/TEAM_SLUG/discussions/42</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">org</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'org'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">team_slug</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'team_slug'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">discussion_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p>
