       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="update-a-discussion" class="pt-3"> <a href="#update-a-discussion">Update a discussion</a> </h3> 
         <p>Edits the title and body text of a discussion post. Only the parameters you provide are updated. OAuth access tokens require the <code>write:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>PATCH /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="update-a-discussion--parameters"> <a href="#update-a-discussion--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#update-a-discussion-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>discussion_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>title</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The discussion post's title.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>body</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The discussion post's body text.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="update-a-discussion--code-samples"> <a href="#update-a-discussion--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X PATCH \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/teams/TEAM_SLUG/discussions/42 \
  -d '{"title":"title"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'PATCH /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">org</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'org'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">team_slug</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'team_slug'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">discussion_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'title'</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <h4 id="update-a-discussion-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="delete-a-discussion" class="pt-3"> <a href="#delete-a-discussion">Delete a discussion</a> </h3> 
         <p>Delete a discussion from a team's page. OAuth access tokens require the <code>write:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>DELETE /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="delete-a-discussion--parameters"> <a href="#delete-a-discussion--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>discussion_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="delete-a-discussion--code-samples"> <a href="#delete-a-discussion--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X DELETE \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/teams/TEAM_SLUG/discussions/42</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'DELETE /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">org</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'org'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">team_slug</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'team_slug'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">discussion_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 204 No Content</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-discussions-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-discussions-legacy">List discussions (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#list-discussions"><code>List discussions</code></a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>List all discussions on a team's page. OAuth access tokens require the <code>read:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /teams/{team_id}/discussions</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-discussions-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#list-discussions-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#list-discussions-legacy-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>direction</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>One of <code>asc</code> (ascending) or <code>desc</code> (descending).</p> Default: <code>desc</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p>

          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-a-discussion-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-a-discussion-legacy">Create a discussion (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#create-a-discussion"><code>Create a discussion</code></a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Creates a new discussion post on a team's page. OAuth access tokens require the <code>write:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p>This endpoint triggers <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/managing-subscriptions-and-notifications-on-github/about-notifications">notifications</a>. Creating content too quickly using this endpoint may result in abuse rate limiting. See "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#abuse-rate-limits">Abuse rate limits</a>" and "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/guides/best-practices-for-integrators#dealing-with-rate-limits">Dealing with abuse rate limits</a>" for details.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /teams/{team_id}/discussions</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-a-discussion-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#create-a-discussion-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#create-a-discussion-legacy-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>title</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The discussion post's title.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>body</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The discussion post's body text.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>private</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">boolean</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Private posts are only visible to team members, organization owners, and team maintainers. Public posts are visible to all members of the organization. Set to <code>true</code> to create a private post.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="create-a-discussion-legacy--code-samples"> <a href="#create-a-discussion-legacy--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/teams/42/discussions \
  -d '{"title":"title","body":"body"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'POST /teams/{team_id}/discussions'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">team_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'title'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">body</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'body'</span>
})
</code></pre>

         </div>

         <h4 id="create-a-discussion-legacy-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div>

         <h3 id="get-a-discussion-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-a-discussion-legacy">Get a discussion (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#get-a-discussion">Get a discussion</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Get a specific discussion on a team's page. OAuth access tokens require the <code>read:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /teams/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}</code></pre>

         <h3 id="update-a-discussion-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#update-a-discussion-legacy">Update a discussion (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#update-a-discussion">Update a discussion</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Edits the title and body text of a discussion post. Only the parameters you provide are updated. OAuth access tokens require the <code>write:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /teams/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}</code></pre>

       <h2 id="discussion-comments"><a href="#discussion-comments">Discussion comments</a></h2> 
       <p>The team discussion comments API allows you to get, create, edit, and delete discussion comments on a <a href="/en/rest/reference/teams#discussions">team discussion</a> post. Any member of the team's <a href="/en/rest/reference/orgs">organization</a> can create and read comments on a public discussion. For more details, see "<a href="/en/organizations/collaborating-with-your-team/about-team-discussions">About team discussions</a>." This API is only available to authenticated members of the team's organization.</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-discussion-comments" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-discussion-comments">List discussion comments</a> </h3> 
         <p>List all comments on a team discussion. OAuth access tokens require the <code>read:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>GET /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-discussion-comments--parameters"> <a href="#list-discussion-comments--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#list-discussion-comments-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>discussion_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>direction</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>One of <code>asc</code> (ascending) or <code>desc</code> (descending).</p> Default: <code>desc</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <h4 id="list-discussion-comments-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-a-discussion-comment" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-a-discussion-comment">Create a discussion comment</a> </h3> 
         <p>Creates a new comment on a team discussion. OAuth access tokens require the <code>write:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p>This endpoint triggers <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/managing-subscriptions-and-notifications-on-github/about-notifications">notifications</a>. Creating content too quickly using this endpoint may result in abuse rate limiting. See "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#abuse-rate-limits">Abuse rate limits</a>" and "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/guides/best-practices-for-integrators#dealing-with-rate-limits">Dealing with abuse rate limits</a>" for details.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>POST /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-a-discussion-comment--parameters"> <a href="#create-a-discussion-comment--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#create-a-discussion-comment-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>discussion_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>body</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The discussion comment's body text.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="create-a-discussion-comment--code-samples"> <a href="#create-a-discussion-comment--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4>

         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \

  -d '{"body":"body"}'</code></pre>

         <h3 id="get-a-discussion-comment" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-a-discussion-comment">Get a discussion comment</a> </h3> 
         <p>Get a specific comment on a team discussion. OAuth access tokens require the <code>read:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>GET /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments/{comment_number}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments/{comment_number}</code></pre>

         <h4 id="get-a-discussion-comment-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="update-a-discussion-comment" class="pt-3"> <a href="#update-a-discussion-comment">Update a discussion comment</a> </h3> 
         <p>Edits the body text of a discussion comment. OAuth access tokens require the <code>write:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>PATCH /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments/{comment_number}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments/{comment_number}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="update-a-discussion-comment--parameters"> <a href="#update-a-discussion-comment--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#update-a-discussion-comment-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>discussion_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>comment_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>body</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The discussion comment's body text.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="update-a-discussion-comment--code-samples"> <a href="#update-a-discussion-comment--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X PATCH \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/teams/TEAM_SLUG/discussions/42/comments/42 \
  -d '{"body":"body"}'</code></pre>

         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'PATCH /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments/{comment_number}'</span>, {

  <span class="hljs-attr">team_slug</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'team_slug'</span>,

  <span class="hljs-attr">comment_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,

})

         <h3 id="delete-a-discussion-comment" class="pt-3"> <a href="#delete-a-discussion-comment">Delete a discussion comment</a> </h3> 
         <p>Deletes a comment on a team discussion. OAuth access tokens require the <code>write:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>DELETE /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments/{comment_number}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments/{comment_number}</code></pre>

         <h3 id="list-discussion-comments-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-discussion-comments-legacy">List discussion comments (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#list-discussion-comments">List discussion comments</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>List all comments on a team discussion. OAuth access tokens require the <code>read:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /teams/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-discussion-comments-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#list-discussion-comments-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#list-discussion-comments-legacy-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>discussion_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>direction</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>One of <code>asc</code> (ascending) or <code>desc</code> (descending).</p> Default: <code>desc</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td>

           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td>

            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td>

         <h4 id="list-discussion-comments-legacy--code-samples"> <a href="#list-discussion-comments-legacy--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \

         <h4 id="list-discussion-comments-legacy-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-a-discussion-comment-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-a-discussion-comment-legacy">Create a discussion comment (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#create-a-discussion-comment">Create a discussion comment</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Creates a new comment on a team discussion. OAuth access tokens require the <code>write:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
         <p>This endpoint triggers <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/managing-subscriptions-and-notifications-on-github/about-notifications">notifications</a>. Creating content too quickly using this endpoint may result in abuse rate limiting. See "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#abuse-rate-limits">Abuse rate limits</a>" and "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/guides/best-practices-for-integrators#dealing-with-rate-limits">Dealing with abuse rate limits</a>" for details.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /teams/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-a-discussion-comment-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#create-a-discussion-comment-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#create-a-discussion-comment-legacy-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>discussion_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>body</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The discussion comment's body text.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

         <h3 id="get-a-discussion-comment-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-a-discussion-comment-legacy">Get a discussion comment (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#get-a-discussion-comment">Get a discussion comment</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Get a specific comment on a team discussion. OAuth access tokens require the <code>read:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /teams/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments/{comment_number}</code></pre> 
        <div>

           </tr>

         <h4 id="get-a-discussion-comment-legacy-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="update-a-discussion-comment-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#update-a-discussion-comment-legacy">Update a discussion comment (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#update-a-discussion-comment">Update a discussion comment</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Edits the body text of a discussion comment. OAuth access tokens require the <code>write:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /teams/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments/{comment_number}</code></pre> 
        <div>

           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_id</code></td>

         <h3 id="delete-a-discussion-comment-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#delete-a-discussion-comment-legacy">Delete a discussion comment (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#delete-a-discussion-comment">Delete a discussion comment</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Deletes a comment on a team discussion. OAuth access tokens require the <code>write:discussion</code> <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/">scope</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /teams/{team_id}/discussions/{discussion_number}/comments/{comment_number}</code></pre>

       <h2 id="members"><a href="#members">Members</a></h2> 
       <p>This API is only available to authenticated members of the team's organization. OAuth access tokens require the <code>read:org</code> <a href="/en/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps">scope</a>.</p> 
       <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
        <p><strong>Note:</strong> When you have team synchronization set up for a team with your organization's identity provider (IdP), you will see an error if you attempt to use the API for making changes to the team's membership. If you have access to manage group membership in your IdP, you can manage GitHub team membership through your identity provider, which automatically adds and removes team members in an organization. For more information, see "<a href="/en/organizations/managing-saml-single-sign-on-for-your-organization/managing-team-synchronization-for-your-organization" class="dotcom-only">Synchronizing teams between your identity provider and GitHub</a>."</p> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-pending-team-invitations" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-pending-team-invitations">List pending team invitations</a> </h3> 
         <p>The return hash contains a <code>role</code> field which refers to the Organization Invitation role and will be one of the following values: <code>direct_member</code>, <code>admin</code>, <code>billing_manager</code>, <code>hiring_manager</code>, or <code>reinstate</code>. If the invitee is not a GitHub member, the <code>login</code> field in the return hash will be <code>null</code>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>GET /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/invitations</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/invitations</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-pending-team-invitations--parameters"> <a href="#list-pending-team-invitations--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td>

         <h3 id="list-team-members" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-team-members">List team members</a> </h3> 
         <p>Team members will include the members of child teams.</p> 
         <p>To list members in a team, the team must be visible to the authenticated user.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/members</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-team-members--parameters"> <a href="#list-team-members--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-team-membership-for-a-user" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-team-membership-for-a-user">Get team membership for a user</a> </h3> 
         <p>Team members will include the members of child teams.</p> 
         <p>To get a user's membership with a team, the team must be visible to the authenticated user.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>GET /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/memberships/{username}</code>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> The response contains the <code>state</code> of the membership and the member's <code>role</code>.</p> 
         <p>The <code>role</code> for organization owners is set to <code>maintainer</code>. For more information about <code>maintainer</code> roles, see see <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#create-a-team">Create a team</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/memberships/{username}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-team-membership-for-a-user--parameters"> <a href="#get-team-membership-for-a-user--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr>

            <td class="opacity-70">string</td>

         <h3 id="add-or-update-team-membership-for-a-user" class="pt-3"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-membership-for-a-user">Add or update team membership for a user</a> </h3> 
         <p>Team synchronization is available for organizations using GitHub Enterprise Cloud. For more information, see <a href="https://help.github.com/github/getting-started-with-github/githubs-products">GitHub's products</a> in the GitHub Help documentation.</p> 
         <p>Adds an organization member to a team. An authenticated organization owner or team maintainer can add organization members to a team.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> When you have team synchronization set up for a team with your organization's identity provider (IdP), you will see an error if you attempt to use the API for making changes to the team's membership. If you have access to manage group membership in your IdP, you can manage GitHub team membership through your identity provider, which automatically adds and removes team members in an organization. For more information, see "<a href="https://help.github.com/articles/synchronizing-teams-between-your-identity-provider-and-github/">Synchronizing teams between your identity provider and GitHub</a>."</p> 
         <p>An organization owner can add someone who is not part of the team's organization to a team. When an organization owner adds someone to a team who is not an organization member, this endpoint will send an invitation to the person via email. This newly-created membership will be in the "pending" state until the person accepts the invitation, at which point the membership will transition to the "active" state and the user will be added as a member of the team.</p> 
         <p>If the user is already a member of the team, this endpoint will update the role of the team member's role. To update the membership of a team member, the authenticated user must be an organization owner or a team maintainer.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>PUT /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/memberships/{username}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/memberships/{username}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="add-or-update-team-membership-for-a-user--parameters"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-membership-for-a-user--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

          -->

           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>team_slug parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>username</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>role</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The role that this user should have in the team. Can be one of:<br> * <code>member</code> - a normal member of the team.<br> * <code>maintainer</code> - a team maintainer. Able to add/remove other team members, promote other team members to team maintainer, and edit the team's name and description.</p> Default: <code>member</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="add-or-update-team-membership-for-a-user--code-samples"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-membership-for-a-user--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4>

         <h3 id="remove-team-membership-for-a-user" class="pt-3"> <a href="#remove-team-membership-for-a-user">Remove team membership for a user</a> </h3> 
         <p>Team synchronization is available for organizations using GitHub Enterprise Cloud. For more information, see <a href="https://help.github.com/github/getting-started-with-github/githubs-products">GitHub's products</a> in the GitHub Help documentation.</p> 
         <p>To remove a membership between a user and a team, the authenticated user must have 'admin' permissions to the team or be an owner of the organization that the team is associated with. Removing team membership does not delete the user, it just removes their membership from the team.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> When you have team synchronization set up for a team with your organization's identity provider (IdP), you will see an error if you attempt to use the API for making changes to the team's membership. If you have access to manage group membership in your IdP, you can manage GitHub team membership through your identity provider, which automatically adds and removes team members in an organization. For more information, see "<a href="https://help.github.com/articles/synchronizing-teams-between-your-identity-provider-and-github/">Synchronizing teams between your identity provider and GitHub</a>."</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>DELETE /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/memberships/{username}</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/memberships/{username}</code></pre> 
        <div>

         <h3 id="list-pending-team-invitations-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-pending-team-invitations-legacy">List pending team invitations (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#list-pending-team-invitations"><code>List pending team invitations</code></a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>The return hash contains a <code>role</code> field which refers to the Organization Invitation role and will be one of the following values: <code>direct_member</code>, <code>admin</code>, <code>billing_manager</code>, <code>hiring_manager</code>, or <code>reinstate</code>. If the invitee is not a GitHub member, the <code>login</code> field in the return hash will be <code>null</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /teams/{team_id}/invitations</code></pre> 
        <div>

         <h3 id="list-team-members-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-team-members-legacy">List team members (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#list-team-members"><code>List team members</code></a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Team members will include the members of child teams.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /teams/{team_id}/members</code></pre>

         <h3 id="get-team-member-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-team-member-legacy">Get team member (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p>The "Get team member" endpoint (described below) is deprecated.</p> 
         <p>We recommend using the <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#get-team-membership-for-a-user">Get team membership for a user</a> endpoint instead. It allows you to get both active and pending memberships.</p> 
         <p>To list members in a team, the team must be visible to the authenticated user.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /teams/{team_id}/members/{username}</code></pre>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="add-team-member-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#add-team-member-legacy">Add team member (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p>The "Add team member" endpoint (described below) is deprecated.</p> 
         <p>We recommend using the <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#add-or-update-team-membership-for-a-user">Add or update team membership for a user</a> endpoint instead. It allows you to invite new organization members to your teams.</p> 
         <p>Team synchronization is available for organizations using GitHub Enterprise Cloud. For more information, see <a href="https://help.github.com/github/getting-started-with-github/githubs-products">GitHub's products</a> in the GitHub Help documentation.</p> 
         <p>To add someone to a team, the authenticated user must be an organization owner or a team maintainer in the team they're changing. The person being added to the team must be a member of the team's organization.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> When you have team synchronization set up for a team with your organization's identity provider (IdP), you will see an error if you attempt to use the API for making changes to the team's membership. If you have access to manage group membership in your IdP, you can manage GitHub team membership through your identity provider, which automatically adds and removes team members in an organization. For more information, see "<a href="https://help.github.com/articles/synchronizing-teams-between-your-identity-provider-and-github/">Synchronizing teams between your identity provider and GitHub</a>."</p> 
         <p>Note that you'll need to set <code>Content-Length</code> to zero when calling out to this endpoint. For more information, see "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#http-verbs">HTTP verbs</a>."</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /teams/{team_id}/members/{username}</code></pre> 
        <div>

         <h3 id="remove-team-member-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#remove-team-member-legacy">Remove team member (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p>The "Remove team member" endpoint (described below) is deprecated.</p> 
         <p>We recommend using the <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#remove-team-membership-for-a-user">Remove team membership for a user</a> endpoint instead. It allows you to remove both active and pending memberships.</p> 
         <p>Team synchronization is available for organizations using GitHub Enterprise Cloud. For more information, see <a href="https://help.github.com/github/getting-started-with-github/githubs-products">GitHub's products</a> in the GitHub Help documentation.</p> 
         <p>To remove a team member, the authenticated user must have 'admin' permissions to the team or be an owner of the org that the team is associated with. Removing a team member does not delete the user, it just removes them from the team.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> When you have team synchronization set up for a team with your organization's identity provider (IdP), you will see an error if you attempt to use the API for making changes to the team's membership. If you have access to manage group membership in your IdP, you can manage GitHub team membership through your identity provider, which automatically adds and removes team members in an organization. For more information, see "<a href="https://help.github.com/articles/synchronizing-teams-between-your-identity-provider-and-github/">Synchronizing teams between your identity provider and GitHub</a>."</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /teams/{team_id}/members/{username}</code></pre>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-team-membership-for-a-user-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-team-membership-for-a-user-legacy">Get team membership for a user (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#get-team-membership-for-a-user">Get team membership for a user</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Team members will include the members of child teams.</p> 
         <p>To get a user's membership with a team, the team must be visible to the authenticated user.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> The response contains the <code>state</code> of the membership and the member's <code>role</code>.</p> 
         <p>The <code>role</code> for organization owners is set to <code>maintainer</code>. For more information about <code>maintainer</code> roles, see <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#create-a-team">Create a team</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /teams/{team_id}/memberships/{username}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-team-membership-for-a-user-legacy--parameters"> <a href="#get-team-membership-for-a-user-legacy--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td>

         <h3 id="add-or-update-team-membership-for-a-user-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#add-or-update-team-membership-for-a-user-legacy">Add or update team membership for a user (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#add-or-update-team-membership-for-a-user">Add or update team membership for a user</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Team synchronization is available for organizations using GitHub Enterprise Cloud. For more information, see <a href="https://help.github.com/github/getting-started-with-github/githubs-products">GitHub's products</a> in the GitHub Help documentation.</p> 
         <p>If the user is already a member of the team's organization, this endpoint will add the user to the team. To add a membership between an organization member and a team, the authenticated user must be an organization owner or a team maintainer.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> When you have team synchronization set up for a team with your organization's identity provider (IdP), you will see an error if you attempt to use the API for making changes to the team's membership. If you have access to manage group membership in your IdP, you can manage GitHub team membership through your identity provider, which automatically adds and removes team members in an organization. For more information, see "<a href="https://help.github.com/articles/synchronizing-teams-between-your-identity-provider-and-github/">Synchronizing teams between your identity provider and GitHub</a>."</p> 
         <p>If the user is unaffiliated with the team's organization, this endpoint will send an invitation to the user via email. This newly-created membership will be in the "pending" state until the user accepts the invitation, at which point the membership will transition to the "active" state and the user will be added as a member of the team. To add a membership between an unaffiliated user and a team, the authenticated user must be an organization owner.</p> 
         <p>If the user is already a member of the team, this endpoint will update the role of the team member's role. To update the membership of a team member, the authenticated user must be an organization owner or a team maintainer.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /teams/{team_id}/memberships/{username}</code></pre> 
        <div>

         <h3 id="remove-team-membership-for-a-user-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#remove-team-membership-for-a-user-legacy">Remove team membership for a user (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#remove-team-membership-for-a-user">Remove team membership for a user</a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Team synchronization is available for organizations using GitHub Enterprise Cloud. For more information, see <a href="https://help.github.com/github/getting-started-with-github/githubs-products">GitHub's products</a> in the GitHub Help documentation.</p> 
         <p>To remove a membership between a user and a team, the authenticated user must have 'admin' permissions to the team or be an owner of the organization that the team is associated with. Removing team membership does not delete the user, it just removes their membership from the team.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> When you have team synchronization set up for a team with your organization's identity provider (IdP), you will see an error if you attempt to use the API for making changes to the team's membership. If you have access to manage group membership in your IdP, you can manage GitHub team membership through your identity provider, which automatically adds and removes team members in an organization. For more information, see "<a href="https://help.github.com/articles/synchronizing-teams-between-your-identity-provider-and-github/">Synchronizing teams between your identity provider and GitHub</a>."</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /teams/{team_id}/memberships/{username}</code></pre>

       <h2 id="team-synchronization"><a href="#team-synchronization">Team synchronization</a></h2> 
       <p>The Team Synchronization API allows you to manage connections between GitHub teams and external identity provider (IdP) groups. To use this API, the authenticated user must be a team maintainer or an owner of the organization associated with the team. The token you use to authenticate will also need to be authorized for use with your IdP (SSO) provider. For more information, see "<a href="/en/github/authenticating-to-github/authorizing-a-personal-access-token-for-use-with-saml-single-sign-on" class="dotcom-only">Authorizing a personal access token for use with a SAML single sign-on organization</a>."</p> 
       <p>You can manage GitHub team members through your IdP with team synchronization. Team synchronization must be enabled to use the Team Synchronization API. For more information, see "<a href="/en/organizations/managing-saml-single-sign-on-for-your-organization/managing-team-synchronization-for-your-organization" class="dotcom-only">Synchronizing teams between your identity provider and GitHub</a>."</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-idp-groups-for-an-organization" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-idp-groups-for-an-organization">List IdP groups for an organization</a> </h3> 
         <p>Team synchronization is available for organizations using GitHub Enterprise Cloud. For more information, see <a href="https://help.github.com/github/getting-started-with-github/githubs-products">GitHub's products</a> in the GitHub Help documentation.</p> 
         <p>List IdP groups available in an organization. You can limit your page results using the <code>per_page</code> parameter. GitHub generates a url-encoded <code>page</code> token using a cursor value for where the next page begins. For more information on cursor pagination, see "<a href="https://dev.to/jackmarchant/offset-and-cursor-pagination-explained-b89">Offset and Cursor Pagination explained</a>."</p> 
         <p>The <code>per_page</code> parameter provides pagination for a list of IdP groups the authenticated user can access in an organization. For example, if the user <code>octocat</code> wants to see two groups per page in <code>octo-org</code> via cURL, it would look like this:</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/team-sync/groups</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-idp-groups-for-an-organization--parameters"> <a href="#list-idp-groups-for-an-organization--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead>

            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr>

          -->

           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td>

            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-or-update-idp-group-connections" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-or-update-idp-group-connections">Create or update IdP group connections</a> </h3> 
         <p>Team synchronization is available for organizations using GitHub Enterprise Cloud. For more information, see <a href="https://help.github.com/github/getting-started-with-github/githubs-products">GitHub's products</a> in the GitHub Help documentation.</p> 
         <p>Creates, updates, or removes a connection between a team and an IdP group. When adding groups to a team, you must include all new and existing groups to avoid replacing existing groups with the new ones. Specifying an empty <code>groups</code> array will remove all connections for a team.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note:</strong> You can also specify a team by <code>org_id</code> and <code>team_id</code> using the route <code>PATCH /organizations/{org_id}/team/{team_id}/team-sync/group-mappings</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /orgs/{org}/teams/{team_slug}/team-sync/group-mappings</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-or-update-idp-group-connections--parameters"> <a href="#create-or-update-idp-group-connections--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented

         <h3 id="create-or-update-idp-group-connections-legacy" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-or-update-idp-group-connections-legacy">Create or update IdP group connections (Legacy)</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> This endpoint route is deprecated and will be removed from the Teams API. We recommend migrating your existing code to use the new <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/teams#create-or-update-idp-group-connections"><code>Create or update IdP group connections</code></a> endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Team synchronization is available for organizations using GitHub Enterprise Cloud. For more information, see <a href="https://help.github.com/github/getting-started-with-github/githubs-products">GitHub's products</a> in the GitHub Help documentation.</p> 
         <p>Creates, updates, or removes a connection between a team and an IdP group. When adding groups to a team, you must include all new and existing groups to avoid replacing existing groups with the new ones. Specifying an empty <code>groups</code> array will remove all connections for a team.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /teams/{team_id}/team-sync/group-mappings</code></pre> 
        <div>
